FreeBSD Ports: Net-im
=====================

Maintainer Requires

--------------

Instant messaging software.
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

**\ `pidgin-libnotify-0.14\_12 <https://svnweb.FreeBSD.org/ports/head/net-im/pidgin-libnotify>`__**
    | This plugin adds a libnotify interface to Pidgin
    | `Long
      description <https://svnweb.FreeBSD.org/ports/head/net-im/pidgin-libnotify/pkg-descr?revision=HEAD>`__
      \|
      `Changes <https://svnweb.FreeBSD.org/ports/head/net-im/pidgin-libnotify/?view=log>`__
